“中美贸易战”文本数据清理¶

In [5]:
str1 = ','.join(col6[1:41])##合并字符串
str2 = ','.join(col6[42:363])
str3 = ','.join(col6[364:513])
str4 = ','.join(col6[514:560])
In [6]:
str1_1 = re.sub("[A-Za-z0-9\!\%\[\]\，\,\。\：\！\、\“\”\（\）\.\/\？\【\】\……\；\——\《\》\' '\■\↓\▲]", "", str1)
str2_1 = re.sub("[A-Za-z0-9\!\%\[\]\，\,\。\：\！\、\“\”\（\）\.\/\？\【\】\……\；\——\《\》\' '\■\↓\▲]", "", str2)
str3_1 = re.sub("[A-Za-z0-9\!\%\[\]\，\,\。\：\！\、\“\”\（\）\.\/\？\【\】\……\；\——\《\》\' '\■\↓\▲]", "", str3)
str4_1 = re.sub("[A-Za-z0-9\!\%\[\]\，\,\。\：\！\、\“\”\（\）\.\/\？\【\】\……\；\——\《\》\' '\■\↓\▲]", "", str4)

  • 4月下旬关键词
In [10]:

keys={}
keys['1'] = str1_1_word
keys['2'] = str2_1_word
keys['3'] = str3_1_word
keys['4'] = str4_1_word

写出不同时段的中美贸易战关键词¶

In [11]:
workbook = xlwt.Workbook(encoding='utf-8')       #打开一个工作簿，编码为utf-8
worksheet = workbook.add_sheet(u'china_daily')
worksheet.write(0, 0, '3月下旬')
worksheet.write(0, 1, '4月上旬')
worksheet.write(0, 2, '4月中旬')
worksheet.write(0, 3, '4月下旬')
for key, value in keys.items():
    for i in list(range(15)):
        worksheet.write(i+1, int(key)-1, value[i])
workbook.save('keys.xls')

TF-IDF计算关键词权重¶

加载需要的包¶

In [12]:
import csv
from sklearn import feature_extraction
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfTransformer
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import CountVectorizer
In [13]:
seg_list_1 = jieba.cut(str1_1)
seg_list_2 = jieba.cut(str2_1)
seg_list_3 = jieba.cut(str3_1)
seg_list_4 = jieba.cut(str4_1)

data1 = " ".join(seg_list_1)
data2 = " ".join(seg_list_2)
data3 = " ".join(seg_list_3)
data4 = " ".join(seg_list_4)

data=[data1,data2,data3,data4]
In [14]:
#将得到的词语转换为词频矩阵
freWord = CountVectorizer()
#统计每个词语的tf-idf权值
transformer = TfidfTransformer()
In [15]:
#计算出tf-idf(第一个fit_transform),并将其转换为tf-idf矩阵(第二个fit_transformer)
tfidf = transformer.fit_transform(freWord.fit_transform(data))
In [16]:
#获取词袋模型中的所有词语
word = freWord.get_feature_names()
#得到权重
weight = tfidf.toarray()
In [17]:
# 直接打印
for i in range(len(weight)):#打印每类文本的tf-idf词语权重，第一个for遍历所有文本，第二个for遍历某一类文本下的词语权重  
    print(u"-------这里输出第",i+1,u"个时间段的词语tf-idf权重------")
    for j in range(len(word)):  
        print(word[j],weight[i][j])

dic={}
for i in range(len(weight)):#打印每类文本的tf-idf词语权重，第一个for遍历所有文本，第二个for遍历某一类文本下的词语权重

        dic[word[j]] = weight[i][j]
